posted:Posted August 30, 2023
msg:Nice hotel next to Tuanjie Xincun Metro Station Line 2, but not up to 5star level. We stayed for 3 nights, as I had prepaid. No English spoken either at the front desk or breakfast cafe. Room was on the 26th floor with a magnificent view looking South. Quiet room, smallish and with little hanging space and no safety box. Breakfast was Chinese and underwhelming. Nice indoor heated pool, but quite crowded with outsiders allowed to swim there. Fantastic gym with everything you could need and all to yourself. Probably stay here again for one night if the price was right. As a day trip, we went to Bingling Si. Take Metro to QiLiHe station on line 1. Walk east past KFC, take the 2nd pedestrian overpass, turn right then left after the touts near the public toilets. This is the Lanzhou West Bus Station. We caught the 9am bus for 23 yuan cash only and only available on the day. At the other end, organised a car for 4 people for 320 yuan. Last bus back at 5:30. It will leave earlier if full. Near QiLiHe station, great coffee place at 76 Jian Gong Xi Jie. Back from the bus station, past KFC, past Metro, left into Jian Gong Xi Jie. Try the 'dirty coffee '

msg:I have been to Gannan ******* Autonomous Prefecture for several days to inspect the project. Yesterday, I returned to Lanzhou after the trip. I chose a hotel close to Lanzhou Railway Station on Ctrip. To be honest, I have traveled all over the country and stayed in almost all kinds of hotels. Lanmei Yihua really made me feel different.
Nowadays, many hotel lobby services are basically zero, and there are only 2-3 staff at the front desk to check in. But I want to say that all the staff in the lobby of this hotel really provide the best service. When you step into the door of the hotel, you will see a staff member smiling at you (and then ask you what help you need). I told him that I booked a hotel. He took the luggage in my hand very kindly and led me to the front desk to help me check in. After checking in, he led me to the elevator. He watched the elevator door close until the elevator came and told me the card swiping location. I guess this big boy should be the lobby manager.
Also, the front desk staff of the hotel did not waste any time in registration, card opening, and identity verification. They were very skilled in their work. What is worth mentioning is that they would tell you everything you wanted to ask without asking, such as what kind of room did you book and what was included, what time and location of afternoon tea (check-in in the afternoon), what time and location of breakfast, and where the wife in the room was behind the room card holder. I feel that this is service, and it is comprehensive. Many standard five-star hotels do this. I hope you work smoothly and happily.
The hotel has a good location, a reasonable and clean interior layout, dry and wet separation, clean and odorless linens, one soft and one hard pillow, and a comfortable mattress.
